# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Bracelets
- Rarity: Uncommon
- Gear Type: Hands
- Color: Red
- Stat Buffs
    - Resell Value = x1.5
    - Damage Plus ✦ = L÷3
- Actives:
    - [Push and Pull](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Push+and+Pull)

- Essence Value: 1000
- Credit Value: 100
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)
